0x000c	0x3f0c	;Form Feed
0x000d	0x3f0d	;Carriage Return
0x000e	0x3f0e	;Shift Out
0x000f	0x3f0f	;Shift In
0x0010	0x3f10	;Data Link Escape
0x0011	0x3f11	;Device Control One
0x0012	0x3f12	;Device Control Two
0x0013	0x3f13	;Device Control Three
0x0014	0x3f3c	;Device Control Four
0x0015	0x3f3d	;Negative Acknowledge

0x0017	0x3f26	;End Of Transmission Block
0x0018	0x3f18	;Cancel
0x0019	0x3f19	;End Of Medium
0x001a	0x3f3f	;Substitute
0x001b	0x3f27	;Escape
0x001c	0x3f1c	;File Separator
